Discourse Two 172

— Tao Zaidong

Numbers from one to ten, hundred, thousand, and ten thousand all represent a fixed quantity. They are rigid and definite, and nothing can replace them. However, the number "two" is different. Sometimes we see "pair," "double," "repeat," "again," "inserted," and "combined" words challenging its position. As a result, the word "two" loses its ability to govern. It is common to overlook this through habit, but once pointed out, it becomes quite interesting. For example, when counting hours, we say "one o'clock" and "two o'clock," but we don't say "two o'clock." However, when it comes to twelve o'clock, we can't say "ten-two o'clock." When counting people using "ge," the Tang poem says, "Two orioles sing amid the willow branches." A common saying is, "Two monks have water to carry." We can't say "two ge." The two hands, two feet, two eyebrows, two eyes, and two ears of the human body can all be referred to as "double," but never "two." If you offer something with both hands, you say "present with both hands," not "present with two hands." We say "frowning with both eyebrows," not "frowning with two eyebrows." When referring to people, we say "a couple" or "a pair of brothers," "two sisters," "two sisters-in-law," or "two daughters-in-law," but in reality, it's always two people. When referring to places, we say "two rivers," "two major rivers," "two lakes," "Guangdong and Guangxi," "Zhejiang and Jiangsu," or "Sichuan." Other examples include a snake with two heads, a horse with two companions, a bow with two stones, a boat with two oars, a temple with two pillars, a house with two corridors, a dress with two sleeves, and a hairpin with two prongs. Nothing can be both great. You can't have both. Events branch in two directions. Intentions can be two-sided. Movement leads to two losses. Combination causes two injuries. All these belong to the meaning of "two," but the word "two" is absolutely not used. National Day, October 10th, is celebrated as the "Twentieth," but we don't call it the "Twentieth Festival," but rather the "Double Tenth Festival." As for the ninth day of the ninth month, we call it "Double Ninth" or "Double Yang," not "Two Nines" or "Two Yangs." "Double" and "repeat" are used instead of "two." One, two, and three are naturally sequential numbers. However, in the I Ching's Meng Hexagram, "the first divination is clear, repeated divinations are annoying," we say "repeated divinations," not "two-three divinations." Ji Wenzi thought three times before acting, and Confucius responded, "Two thoughts are enough," but we say "think again." Therefore, the word "two" is also invaded by the word "again" in some parts. For example, "once and again," "again and again," "think over and over again," "consider carefully again and again," "repeatedly remind," as well as various "rebirths," "re-creations," "re-comings," and "re-attempts," all convey the meaning of "two." This is similar to the phrases "three words and two sentences" in writing, "three cups and two small cups" of wine, and "two or three branches of peach blossoms outside the bamboo," using "two" to replace "two" in a similar way. The lotus has two stems, which could be called "two-stem lotus," but instead, it's called "twin-stem lotus." A boat has two boards, which could be called a "two-board boat," but instead, it's called a "sandwiched-board boat." Instances like these are endless. Why is the word "two" so unfortunate to encounter such entanglement?

Anecdotes from the Painting Academy 173

— Chen Boying

In modern times, among those who paint flowers, the world recognizes Cheng Yaosheng as the best. However, Master Cheng initially had no intention of painting. With his outstanding talent, he unintentionally broke into the field of painting, which is a good story. Master Cheng's name is Zhang, from Huizhou. Many people from Huizhou engage in the pawnshop business, so Master Cheng also entered a pawnshop as an apprentice in his youth. After a while, he realized that the profession was not worth learning. He devoted himself to studying physics and natural sciences, eventually mastering them. He then became a teacher in a school. One day, while teaching about rose flowers, he could not find a specimen. He then showed the students a painting he had made, which he had sketched at a friend's house a month before. When the painting was displayed, the students were amazed by its realism. They then asked him to paint for them, and his colleagues also made requests. Soon, friends and acquaintances heard the news and came to ask for paintings. The paper piled up like a mountain, and he could not fulfill all the requests. Someone said to him, "You are working too hard for others. Why not set a price and limit the number of requests?" Master Cheng followed their advice. Once the price was set, even more people came to ask for paintings, creating a scene like a bustling market in front of his door. As a result, he resigned from his teaching position and devoted himself to painting. He increased his prices every year, but the demand remained the same. A painting of a small size could fetch as much as ten gold pieces.

The Mermaid 174

— Xi Qian

This startling news happened in a small village named Picaoa five years ago. On the outskirts of the town, near the sea, there was a small inn called Panandiss. No one in the nearby population did not know that there were two mermaids in the hotel. One was named Joa Panandiss, and the other was named Baba Panandiss. One day, Qi Erjia Tai (the friend of the inn owner) and him (the owner) talked about politics. He later sat alone at home. All of a sudden, he came back and brought new news: "I saw a beautiful mermaid. Are you happy to go and watch it?" Therefore, they headed to the destination.

On a very clear, moonlit night, a number of villagers were cutting wood along the coast. They stood by Baba's habitat. By the time the night was about to end, only the water of the Atlantic Ocean trickled by itself. The shore was inlaid with a thicket of stones. "Here it comes." They quietly stood up.

One minute, two minutes passed. Nothing was seen. Only the sky that was toppled into the water, the silver moon. Only the sound of splashing water was heard. And then she appeared in the sea. First, the head was seen, along, long hair, draped to the shoulder. The exquisite chest was exposed until the scaly tail. She bent her tail very slowly, sitting on the rocks. She was truly a mermaid.

They were captivated by this water deity of the sea, and discussed the phenomena they had seen. The mermaid heard their voices and quickly dove into the water. And then it was again quiet.

This had happened five years ago. After this, the mermaid had been discovered several times. After this news spread, countless people came to this small hotel to watch. One night, she came again, and brought a companion with her. Ten minutes later, they began to play with each other. The front of the small hotel became like Shanyin Road. A new Panandiss Hotel was built, and the old owner greatly benefited.

For five years, the mermaid of Picaoa attracted customers for the hotel. Night after night, onlookers stood on the shore, hoping to see the beautiful monster. A lot of people only saw a scaly tail in the night, like an ephemeral bloom, and so became greatly disappointed.

But recently, detectives came out. Baba Panandiss was the most strange hoax of modern times. It turns out that the mermaid was his daughter. One night, the mermaid was playing to be watched by the guests. A police ship stealthily sailed out of the harbor. The mermaid heard the sound, and quickly dove into the water. But the police ship waited for them to surface before catching them in one fell swoop. She was indeed the owner's daughter, Tan Lisi. She had a very exquisite fish tail on her leg, and was wearing a nude-colored swimsuit. Her friend was a waitress in the Panandiss hotel.

Because Tan Lisi could swim in the water with her feet together, just like a fish. When the matter was decided, his wife, Malai, made this strange tail. And so this strange event was created.

A Record of Coincidences in a Bandit's Lair 175

— Jian Fu

A guest returned from the Six Counties and recounted the story of a bandit's wife rescuing a hostage. It was quite interesting, so I quickly recorded it to share with readers.

Our county is known for its banditry. The problem with bandits is not so much robbery as it is kidnapping for ransom. The ransom demanded is often enormous, leading to the ruin of even moderately wealthy families. If the family cannot afford to pay, the bandits often kill the hostage and send the body to their door as a warning to those who are stingy with their money. Their cruelty is such. A resident of the county, a wealthy man, had only one son. On the night of his wedding, the bandits heard of it and, armed with weapons, broke down the gate and entered. They looted all the property but were still not satisfied. They then kidnapped his beloved son and left. Afterward, they demanded 20,000 gold pieces for his ransom. The man, deeply concerned for his son, tried his best to raise the money, but in such a short time, it was difficult to gather such a large sum. The bandits suspected him of being stingy and refused to lower the price, so the matter stalled. The bandits repeatedly threatened him, stating in a letter that if the ransom was not paid by the next day, they would kill the hostage. The man, though alarmed, had no way to raise the money and resigned himself to despair. The matter came to the knowledge of the new bride, who, believing that her husband had no hope of returning alive, committed suicide out of grief. Unexpectedly, late that night, the man's son suddenly returned home with a young woman, looking very flustered. The man was overjoyed and eagerly inquired about what had happened. The man's son pointed to the young woman who had come with him and said, "This woman is my savior." He then recounted in detail how he was rescued. It turned out that after the man's son was taken to the bandit's lair, the bandits often went out, leaving only one bandit to guard the hostage. Among them was a female bandit, about twenty years old, with a beautiful appearance. She would occasionally come to visit him, seeming to have deep feelings for him. Over time, they exchanged secret words. She described herself as a native of Yongcheng in Henan, who had also been kidnapped by the bandits. Because the ransom demanded was too high, her family could not afford to pay, so she was trapped among the bandits. As she spoke, she sobbed. The man's son felt sympathy for her but did not dare to believe her. He simply listened to her. That night, the woman suddenly came and told him, "Tonight, all the bandits have gone out as agreed. There is only one bandit guarding the hostage, and he is fast asleep. Is this not a good opportunity for you to escape?" The man's son suspected it was a trap and did not fully trust her. The woman said, "Time is running out." She then took him and fled. After escaping the bandit's lair, the man's son said, "How can I repay you?" The woman said, "I am from a good family and cannot bear to serve bandits. Now that I have escaped the bandit's lair, I have no face to return to my hometown. If you do not despise me, I am willing to entrust my life to you." The man found out her true feelings and was both saddened and happy. Saddened that his daughter-in-law had died, and happy that he had gained a new daughter-in-law. He praised her righteousness and agreed to her request. Fearing retaliation from the bandits, he moved his family to another place, and their whereabouts are unknown.

Warmth in My Heart (377) 176

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 17: Preserving Youth with Skilful Makeup, Continuing Life with Costly Efforts.

Hua Yuanchun stayed in a hotel for ten days after arriving in Beijing. In the Beijing hutongs, this was called "opening the market." The opening days were when the guests would go all out to support the event. Many "red girls" would open the market for ten days consecutively, with a minimum of three days of feasting. Hua Yuanchun, being a famous Shanghai "red girl" and the top attraction at Qingyutang, was given the best room in the front courtyard and told that she would not be seeing guests, as a special case. The manager also instructed the staff to follow Shanghai customs, calling her "Sixth Miss" instead of addressing her as "So-and-so Miss" with her full name. This was to treat her with the preferential treatment afforded to "red girls" from the south. Naturally, a group of wealthy gentlemen would greet and welcome Hua Yuanchun upon her arrival. The opening was supposed to be celebrated with a bang, but unfortunately, she wasn't so lucky. She asked a few acquaintances from Shanghai, but some had already left Beijing for other assignments, and others had already found someone among the girls from the south. They could only offer perfunctory support. She had been expecting Ye Tonghou to arrive within a week, but he was held up by business in Shanghai. Inviting guests in the Beijing hutongs was different from the parlors in Shanghai, where there were people who would gather a crowd or buy tickets. All expenses, such as rickshaw fares and tips for the servants, were borne by the host. Some extravagant friends did not consider the host's finances and would call for three or four girls at once. If all the guests at the table were like that, the expenses for tips alone would be considerable. In addition to the expenses for cars, carriages, and meals for the guests, a feast could easily cost three hundred yuan. Therefore, it was not easy to find someone to invite guests. Hua Yuanchun barely managed to gather three guests, and she made a splash for three days during the opening. This would have been acceptable for ordinary girls, but the pot-bellied manager, who was impressed by Hua Laoliu's reputation as a Shanghai "red girl" and had heard that she had acquaintances in Beijing, thought that she would be able to continue for at least a week. He was somewhat disappointed that it only lasted three days, and that those three days were only perfunctory. However, he still believed that she was new to the north and didn't know many people. He thought that a girl like her would still be popular and wouldn't fall out of favor so quickly. The way of entertaining in Beijing was slightly different from that in Shanghai. Shanghai was, after all, a large commercial center, and even the customers of the brothels had a bit of a commercial smell to them. Therefore, the Masters Zhang and Masters Li were willing to spend money, but they were very shrewd. The money they spent on the girls was commensurate with the situation, just like in business. Beijing society was a political society, with a large number of political figures. They believed in a certain doctrine and devoted all their energy to it. Similarly, when they patronized a girl, they were willing to devote all their energy to it in order to win her favor, they were willing to spend more money. Therefore, for the few popular "red girls" in Beijing, as long as they captured one or two powerful patrons, the rest were insignificant.

▲ Turbulence Continues The gold market on March 7th saw a slight increase in prices, but the volatility remained high, with fluctuations of ten taels in a short period. As a result, market sentiment is shaken, and the price of third-grade yarn is showing signs of fatigue. The previous rumor that local yarn was being shipped to Japan was reportedly false due to non-compliance with packaging requirements, causing market sentiment to retreat further. American Cotton Stable Last Week 185

A telegram from New York on the 6th reports on the cotton market during the past week: trading on the cotton exchange was quiet last week, and prices were mixed. Industry insiders are waiting and watching for new developments. The stability of the political situation in India is enough to improve the cotton goods in Lancashire and Japan, and the domestic demand for cotton cloth continues to be active. These are all reasons for the stability of the market. However, India's proposal to increase the import tax on cotton cloth by 5%, and the German cotton mills' plan to reduce work for six weeks starting on March 16, will also have an impact on the aforementioned situation. When prices rebounded, India and Japan made slight purchases. The issue of reducing cotton planting area is approximately 8% to 15%. It is reported that the cooperative has warned the South that if cotton prices are to improve, the cotton planting area must be reduced to a considerable extent so that supply and demand can be equal. Grain Market: River Downstream Rice Market Turns Firmer 186

▲ Zhabei: Yesterday, over 30 ships arrived from various guilds, and market sales were slightly more active. ▲ Hu Nan: Yesterday, ships from the mainland continued to arrive. The sales market on this street is not good. The white japonica rice market is stable. The source of southern early thin paddy rice is also poor, and the sales channel is not very developed, so prices barely maintain the original level. The xiang rice market is generally flat with few transactions, and the market is quiet. The situation for white yuan rice is mediocre.

Rice Merchants Actively Purchase Xiang Rice 187

Yesterday's xiang rice market situation was quite good. Although merchants from Shantou did not go to warehouses, rice merchants had a very good appetite and purchased a considerable amount in recent days. Yesterday, more than 1,000 bags were sold, and the price immediately rose by 1 to 2 cents. Merchants from Shantou are still inquiring about ke yuan rice, and the market is also firm. This street is also slightly inquiring. The total transaction volume for the day included 325 bags of Jiangxi machine-processed yuan rice, priced at 12.7 yuan to 11.4 yuan, purchased by Shantou merchants. Rice merchants purchased 700 bags of Jiangxi machine-processed late rice, priced at 13 yuan, 12.6 yuan, and 12.3 yuan, respectively. In addition, 200 bags of Hunan machine-processed oil rice were priced at 12.55 yuan, and 100 bags of Jiangxi machine-processed early rice were priced at 12 yuan. 250 bags of Nanjing medium-grade brown rice were priced at 8.7 yuan to 8.4 yuan.

Flour Prices Trend Lower from Flat 188

Yesterday, the flour market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, showed a trend of first stabilizing and then falling for each contract month. The opening prices in the morning were based on quotations for foreign wheat, with little fluctuation. As the weather was not clear, industry insiders and outsiders felt relatively stable. However, in the afternoon, the market atmosphere gradually changed. Spot goods, such as Red and Blue car-branded flour from Naval Transport, can be purchased with a standard increase of 6 cents. As larger factories still have a surplus of foreign wheat, they continue to sell off. The weather also improved and became clear, so prices for each contract month gradually declined. Private sources say that Chicago spot wheat has also been heavily marketed recently, with prices quoted at 19.5 yuan. Factories quote over 18.5 yuan. In addition, Russian wheat is also being marketed, with over 40 varieties of wheat. Judging from this situation, it seems that everything is unfavorable for long positions, so the changes in the future are endless. As a result, the current month contract fell by 1 cent compared to the previous day, the April-May contract fell by 1 cent, the June-July contract fell by 1.5 cents, and the August contract fell by 1.25 cents.

Wheat Futures Market Unanimously Weak 189

Yesterday, the wheat futures market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, showed a downward trend for each contract month. Although the quotations for foreign wheat did not change much, they depended on demand. Factories such as Fuxin and Fufeng have large stockpiles of foreign wheat that are not only sufficient but may even be surplus. The exchange's standards will naturally no longer be purchased. In terms of the environment, it is difficult to stabilize again. Furthermore, the external atmosphere is gradually becoming unfavorable. The marketing of foreign wheat continues unabated, so market sentiment is shaken and prices are gradually softening. As a result, the current month contract fell by 6 cents compared to the previous day, the April contract fell by 4 cents, the May contract fell by 3 cents, the June-July contract fell by 4 cents, and the August contract fell by 3 cents. The spot wheat market is slightly sluggish. 500 bags of Kaidaoren Bridge wheat were priced at 12.623 taels, purchased by Huafeng.

Sugar Market: Raw Sand and White Sugar Slightly Stabilize After Falling 190

Yesterday's sugar market reported that the price of Cuban spot sugar continued to fall by 0.3125 yuan compared to the previous telegram. Only the December contract in New York sugar futures rose by 1 cent, and the remaining months did not fluctuate. The price of Java spot and futures sugar also lacked rising or falling. The association's market delineation, the Dutch sugar No. 24 raw sand and white sugar, due to the lengthening of the exchange rate, prices slumped even further. The initial transaction price was 10.085 taels, with very few buyers and many sellers. Later, the price fell to 10.075 taels, and buyers gradually became more active, with over 1,000 bags traded. Sellers tightened, and the market gradually became firmer. However, it had already fallen sharply by 1.5 cents compared to the previous day. Medium-grade white sugar was quoted at 10.03 taels, with no inquiries. The Japanese sugar market also trended weaker, with even fewer transactions. N-mark was priced at 10.0775 taels, TK mark at 10.075 taels, YT mark at 10.07 taels, YP mark at 10.0975 to 0.095 taels, and YRO mark at 10.045 to 0.04 taels. The market conditions were weak across the board. The board had a consolidated hand of ice, opening dozens of boxes, priced at 8 taels per yuan, and the market was flat and unremarkable.

Youth Corner

Era Youth Society Holds Essay Contest 191

— Wen

Regarding the Era Youth Society, its current position in the youth community has its own general value and weight, which I need not elaborate on here. This can be seen in the "Era Youth" weekly publication. Now, in order to encourage youth academic research and publication abilities, they are holding their first essay contest, titled "Several Important Issues for Era Youth" and "Literature and Art and Politics." The former discusses issues related to youth themselves, while the latter is a review of the current stage of the literary and artistic movement. The society has also prepared cash prizes, with the first prize being 30 yuan, the second prize being 20 yuan, the third prize being 10 yuan, and the fourth to tenth prizes being books, stationery, and other souvenirs. In addition to welcoming submissions from members, non-members are also welcome to participate. It is said that many excellent works have already been received, but for the sake of general consideration, the deadline has not yet been set. The mailing address is c/o West Gate Daguang Bookstore.

Era Youth 192

— Wen

27th Special Large Issue

Daguang Bookstore General Distributor

The youth's field requires the youth's own labor force to engage in the work of reclamation. We can see the entire state revealed by the youth community from the expression of this inner genuine emotion, and at the same time, we can find clues as to why the youth have such requirements in a certain consciousness and occasion. Of course, in recent years, the division of the youth community, the path of decline of the majority of youth, and the creation of a terrifying situation are due to the inability of youth to have mutual trust and shared belief. But is it not also the shackles of the environment that sweep the youth into the whirlpool of hesitation? The youth wandering at the crossroads is indeed a sign of the youth's weak will. However, when it comes to the final analysis, it is often related to the social system. We should also admit it. Therefore, there are inevitably enlightened youth who see through this phenomenon and rise up to defend the entire youth community, on the one hand, pointing out the sins of the status quo, and on the other hand, deeply reflecting on themselves, hoping for general awakening. Thus, the so-called silent zero encirclement is broken through, and we can see its promising path from the sum of the pioneering forces.

We can certainly say that "Era Youth" is the product of this situation because their reasons for launching and development coincide with what was said above. They recognized the meaning of the promotion given to youth by the cycle of the era, stood at the measure of the era to pursue a fulfilling life, were liberated from the cage of disease, and raised their heads towards the realm of light.

In summary, "Era Youth" has been published for almost half a year now. Although we cannot say that it has generated any strength, the fact that they have made unremitting efforts is a very good sign for the youth community, which deserves praise. Now, starting from the 27th issue, the scope has been expanded again, "because we feel that the scope is too small to accommodate as many submissions as possible, so we decided to expand the original scope. Generally, we will still inherit the previous practice, only in the compilation aspect, the editors will do their best to gradually reform." From this, the expansion plan of "Era Youth" has been realized, so we will inevitably be able to see further performance, and win glory for the youth themselves.

Truly, "at whatever new stage, there must be the revealing of the expectation of a new expression, as a tendency to be respected and followed," so we read such a passage in Li Dachun's "New Opening":

... Of course, we always admit that a weak force may only be equal to a trembling groan, but precisely because the environment in which the youth are in is such a tragic situation, especially during this period of rapid change in the great era, the shadows of the decadent twilight obscure the active atmosphere of the entire youth community. On the one hand, due to the historical objective facts, we are even more inevitably unable to settle down, and then we will strive to express the spirit of our era youth, so that our hearts can grasp the comfort of the right track. As a result, we finally lifted our heads from the confinement of the low-spirited atmosphere and moved forward on the path of struggle. Therefore, the main purpose in the future is still to be summed up in this direction. Our explorations are not limited to the narrow definition. All issues that directly or indirectly affect the youth themselves, we need to review for reasonable requirements. In the theory and practice of the youth movement, we will not relax in opening up a bright path, breaking through the crisis of silence and decline. In addition, regarding other things, we have also talked about in the "Publication Preface." In short, for the crystallization of loyalty and enthusiasm, we should earnestly accept and give the opportunity to publish.

... The youth of the era should urgently take on a task. Our pursuit of the project is to think about the way out for the entire youth community. Then, if we do not forget the position we are in at present, the era we are in, we should not hesitate to press the responsibility of nurturing actions on our own shoulders.

Indeed, the past "Era Youth" has had many explorations in the theory and practice of the youth movement. Recently, Hao Wu's "Era Youth and National Movement" has fully elaborated the institutions maintained by the Era Youth and the national movement. Secondly, Li Chunsen's "The Beginning of the 20th Year and the Prospect of the Chinese Youth Movement" more clearly marked the program of action. These are probably well known to readers. In this issue, there is another text worth paying attention to, which is Zhu Jianbai's "Youth and Politics." This issue seems to be broad, but the author's sectional explanation makes us clearly understand the relationship between youth and politics. This is also often the case in texts discussing the youth movement. The efforts of the youth movement are actually actions that directly participate in politics. Whether today's youth movement should directly participate in political actions is an issue worthy of detailed review. The author first solves the two major premises of what is youth and what is politics. Under the titles of politics and youth, he explains the education of politics and youth, the way out of politics and youth, and the activities of politics and youth. Under the titles of youth and politics, he explains the current situation of youth and politics, the revolution of youth and politics, the ideology of youth and politics, and the activities of youth and politics. As for the author's conclusion, he said, "Finally, we must know that youth and politics have an inseparable relationship. If youth do not care about politics, politics will interfere with everything about youth. The current political situation is even more awaiting the improvement of youth. Therefore, the youth should strive for political activities, in principle, there is nothing wrong with it. However, if the youth misinterpret the political ideology, they will go the wrong way in political activities. This must be paid attention to, especially during the period of political tutelage, when the work of destruction has passed and the responsibility of construction is being shouldered. In practice, the direct political activities of students in school have to be restricted. This is precisely to give students in school the opportunity for full preparation, which is a positive intention, not a negative measure..." This is a powerful insight, which we should pay attention to.

In addition, there are also Jing Qi's "The Place of Modern Women under Capitalism and Their Due Self-Awareness," Yi Tie Jun's "The Prospect of Recovering the Shanghai Concession and Revolutionary Diplomacy," Yi Chun's "Relief of the Crisis of Dropping Out of School in the Period of Change," Mo Zhi's "Youth and Reading Clubs," Luo Xiang's "Reflections," Qi Yun's "In the Examination Field," and Yi Wencao's novel "Dumb Old Man," all of which are written with the youth's loyal thoughts. "School Radio" reports the news of various schools. After reading it, we will have an indescribable taste. Such compilation will increase the driving force of the youth of the era.
